- when the user asks for 晨间复盘, follow the fixed order “读取错误日志→读取昨日复盘→按周计划安排→检查审批→检查交易日志” -> restore context in that sequence instead of re-asking for structure [Task 1]

## Reusable knowledge

- `memory/error_log.md` can still be useful on a no-new-error day: keep same-day state as “无新错误”, but list `IndentationError: unexpected indent (server.py:691)`, `9091/9092 venv损坏`, and `OKX API SSL不稳定` under historical carryover / 待复核 instead of promoting them to new incidents [Task 1]
- The effective approvals file for this workflow is `/Users/luxiangnan/edict/data/pending_approvals.json`; in the represented run it showed `pending_count: 0`, while historical black-swan items remained `rejected`, so the morning review did not need an approval-action branch [Task 1]

- `memory/2026-04-30.md` and `memory/learning/self_evolution_2026_q1.md` already aligned the next-day theme to “交易系统综合诊断”, “复盘 PnL 回撤来源”, “检查做空/极度恐慌信号与实盘 ETH/BTC 持仓方向是否一致”, and “形成仓位降噪规则”; the morning review can inherit that line of work directly instead of inventing a new theme [Task 1]

## Failures and how to do differently

- symptom: the morning review checks `pending_approvals.json` in several places and wastes time on empty paths -> cause: there are multiple candidate locations but only `/Users/luxiangnan/edict/data/pending_approvals.json` is authoritative here -> fix: go to that exact path first [Task 1]

- symptom: the review reports only market emotion like “做空/极度恐慌” and misses live account risk -> cause: sentiment was not reconciled against open positions, leverage, and liquidation distance -> fix: treat `.sentiment_latest.json` / sentiment conclusions as one input and explicitly compare them with the live position mix before closing the review [Task 1]

- symptom: parsing `sentiment_pool.json` treats `news` as a flat list and returns misleading empty/newsless results -> cause: the crawler stores items under `news.items` -> fix: inspect `d.get('news', {}).get('items', [])` and then summarize counts from that nested list [Task 3]

### keywords

- even2026.tianlu2026.org, G2 Bridge, Even G2, ocuclaw, openclaw-gateway, localhost:18789, localhost:9000, tunnel.yml, .cloudflared/config.yml, openclaw.json, openclaw.plugin.json, evenAiEnabled, relayToken, wsBind, Unauthorized, codex app-server startup aborted, native hook relay not found

## User preferences

- when the user asks “你现在是什么模型？”, answer it from live session state first instead of giving a long explanation or a guess [Task 1]
- when the user asks “电脑的状态如何？”, give a concise operational conclusion with the main load source and whether anything is actually wrong, not a raw metric dump [Task 2]
- when the user asks whether a domain service or plugin is “正常吗”, treat that as an end-to-end health check -> verify public endpoint, local listener, config, and logs together instead of checking only one surface [Task 3]
- when the user says “能修复一下吗？我这会儿眼镜访问不到open claw了。”, treat it as a live repair request -> change the broken route, restart once, and verify the real glasses reply path instead of only explaining backend health [Task 3]
- when a live restart or verification takes long enough for the user to ask “你怎么了？”, keep status updates short and frequent rather than going silent mid-repair [Task 3]

## Reusable knowledge

- `session_status` is the fastest reliable source for “what model is this session using?” in this environment; the captured reply was `openai-codex/gpt-5.5` with think `medium` [Task 1]
- For quick Mac health checks here, the compact command set `uptime`, `pmset -g batt`, `vm_stat`, `df -h`, `top`, and `memory_pressure` was enough to conclude the machine was broadly healthy while still identifying the real hot spots [Task 2]
- On this host, a common transient heavy CPU source is Spotlight indexing: the captured run found `mds_stores` around `96% CPU`, with `mediaanalysisd`, `openclaw-gateway`, and multiple `freqtrade` processes also active, while `memory_pressure` still showed `System-wide memory free percentage: 52%` [Task 2]
- `even2026.tianlu2026.org` is routed through Cloudflare Tunnel to local `http://localhost:18789`; in the validated check, the public root plus `/health`, `/status`, and `/api/health` all returned the same `{"status":"ok","agent":"G2 Bridge","version":"5.0.0","gateway":true,"telegram":false}` family of health JSON, while unauthorized POST returned `Unauthorized`, so public reachability and auth enforcement were both live [Task 3]
- Local listener roles are split: `127.0.0.1:18789` served the G2 bridge health JSON, while `127.0.0.1:9000` was listening but returned `404 not found` on `/`, `/health`, and `/status`, so lack of an HTTP health page on `9000` is not by itself a failure [Task 3]
- The relevant plugin/config surfaces for Even G2 checks are `plugins.entries.ocuclaw` in `/Users/luxiangnan/.openclaw/openclaw.json` and the corresponding `openclaw.plugin.json`; the captured healthy config included `enabled: true`, `evenAiEnabled: true`, `relayToken`, `evenAiToken`, and `wsBind: 0.0.0.0` [Task 3]
- `~/.openclaw/even-ai-settings.json` is a separate runtime input for OcuClaw Even AI routing; a healthy domain plus healthy `ocuclaw` plugin config is not enough if this file still points `defaultModel` at `minimax2-7/MiniMax-M2.7-highspeed` and `defaultThinking` at `xhigh` [Task 3]
- The runtime error `unexpected status 404 Not Found: 404 page not found, url: https://api.minimaxi.com/v1/responses` is a strong routing clue: the glasses request path reached the wrong provider/API, so the fix belongs in Even AI model settings rather than tunnel health or token-length guessing [Task 3]
- The strongest failure signals for real G2 path issues in this environment were log lines `codex app-server startup aborted` and `native hook relay not found`; these matter more than a healthy domain root if the user is asking whether the glasses bridge is truly working [Task 3]

## Failures and how to do differently

- symptom: an answer about model or machine health becomes overly verbose -> cause: treating a direct status question like a general exploration prompt -> fix: lead with the conclusion, then include only the metrics that justify it [Task 1][Task 2]
- symptom: domain health looks green, but the real Even G2 request path is still broken -> cause: checking only the public URL or local listener and not the upstream plugin/log chain -> fix: cross-check the public endpoint, local ports, plugin config, and gateway/plugin logs before calling the bridge healthy [Task 3]
- symptom: local `127.0.0.1:18789/v1/chat/completions` returns `Unauthorized`, but the user is really asking why the glasses did not receive the reply -> cause: the local POST path sits behind a different auth boundary and is not the final truth for the glasses delivery chain -> fix: use the public Even G2 path plus runtime logs and Even AI settings as the real end-to-end verification targets [Task 3]
- symptom: the first guess centers on token length or restart state, but the public domain and local gateway already look healthy -> cause: the deeper routing file `~/.openclaw/even-ai-settings.json` was not checked yet -> fix: inspect that runtime settings file early, especially after `codex app-server startup aborted` or `api.minimaxi.com/v1/responses` 404s [Task 3]
- symptom: broad grep over `even2026` or `Even G2` produces too much noise -> cause: starting from generic search instead of the known config/log anchors -> fix: narrow quickly to `openclaw.json`, `openclaw.plugin.json`, `tunnel.yml` or `.cloudflared/config.yml`, the live listeners on `18789` and `9000`, and the gateway/plugin logs [Task 3]
- symptom: `localhost:9000` returns `404 not found` on normal HTTP paths -> cause: that port is a relay/WebSocket surface rather than the main bridge health endpoint -> fix: treat `18789` plus the public `even2026` domain as the primary health endpoints and use `9000` only as a listener/config corroboration check [Task 3]

## User preferences

- when this kind of cron task runs, the workflow expected the output file to be checked and the latest state to be recorded in memory -> future runs should verify the written file/state, not stop at the script exit code [Task 1]
- when a cron run is described as “抓取 + 写回”, treat artifact refresh and same-day memory bookkeeping as one completion unit -> do not leave the `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` append as an optional afterthought [Task 1]
- when the cron task is explicitly named `天禄-外部信号自动获取(P2)`, treat that as a cue that the whole job is `抓取 + 写回当日总结`, not just the script execution itself [Task 1]
- when the cron trigger is routine and `alerts` stays empty, default to execute + verify + quiet completion; report only meaningful anomalies instead of narrating routine success or escalating to the user/father [Task 1]
- when the task is framed as “外部信号自动获取(P2)”, default to checking external data-source reachability, fallback behavior, and the latest persisted file state rather than treating it as a fire-and-forget fetch [Task 1]
- when checking this cron family after a long stretch of Binance failures, read the latest saved JSON and memory note before summarizing source health -> do not collapse the result to simply “Binance up/down” without checking the per-field `exchange` tags [Task 1]
- when the cron message already names the script to run, default to direct execution-and-verify workflow rather than a planning discussion [Task 1]
- when this cron family runs, keep the durable sequence `run script -> inspect external_signals.json -> update daily memory` instead of mixing the bookkeeping step into the middle [Task 1]

## Failures and how to do differently

- symptom: a broad timestamp grep such as `14:12\\|14:1[0-9].*P2 外部信号` fails to locate the freshly appended line -> cause: the memory file layout is section-oriented and the loose grep can miss the actual insertion context -> fix: search the section header `^## 外部信号` directly and inspect the nearby lines instead of debugging the append from timestamp grep alone [Task 1]
- symptom: the agent spends time scanning a broad daily-memory range even though the target section is already known -> cause: verification starts from the whole `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` file instead of the named `## 外部信号` block -> fix: jump straight to `^## 外部信号` once the heading is known, then verify the nearby appended line with `grep` or a narrow `sed` window [Task 1]
- symptom: first async/background execution does not immediately show a completed result -> cause: launch status alone does not prove the cron-style script finished and wrote output -> fix: follow with `--status` and direct file read / mtime check before closing the task [Task 1]
- symptom: `external_signals.json` refreshed and `--status` looks healthy, but the current run is still absent from `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` -> cause: `external_signals_fetcher.py` updates the artifact file but does not guarantee the daily-memory writeback step -> fix: treat writeback as a separate completion gate, search `^## 外部信号` in the daily memory file, and patch the missing dated line before closing the cron run [Task 1]
- symptom: `external_signals_fetcher.py` is still running after the first launch check -> cause: this fetcher can be a long-running process even on successful runs -> fix: poll for completion or re-check `Knowledge/external_signals/external_signals.json` mtime and parsed fields after the process exits instead of assuming launch equals completion [Task 1]
- symptom: simple waiting or PID polling does not give a trustworthy completion signal -> cause: the fetcher can finish between checks, and process-state evidence is weaker than the saved artifact for this workflow -> fix: prefer `stat`, `jq`, and `external_signals_fetcher.py --status` as the real completion proof, then verify the dated line in `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` [Task 1]
- symptom: `jq` probing starts before the long-running fetcher has finished writing the file -> cause: verification began against an in-flight refresh, so schema mismatches and stale content are easier to misread -> fix: wait for session/process exit first, then use `python3 -m json.tool` or direct JSON reads before summarizing the saved fields [Task 1]
- symptom: the first read of `external_signals.json` still shows the previous snapshot -> cause: the fetcher had not finished writing yet even though the file was already being checked -> fix: wait for process completion, then re-run `sed`/`stat` or another direct file proof before concluding the artifact did not refresh [Task 1]
- symptom: one saved signal comes from `binance` while another still comes from `gate` -> cause: upstream recovery is partial, so `funding_rate` and `long_short_ratio` do not share one binary reachability state -> fix: inspect and report the saved per-field `exchange` and `source_note` values independently before calling the run full fallback or recovered [Task 1]
- symptom: Binance returns `No route to host` and the saved JSON shows fallback for the affected field -> cause: environment/network reachability issue, not necessarily a script failure -> fix: treat it as non-blocking when Gate fallback is present and `external_signals.json` is populated [Task 1]
- symptom: Binance funding-rate fetch fails with `SSLEOFError(8, 'EOF occurred in violation of protocol (_ssl.c:1129)')` but the file still refreshes -> cause: upstream TLS/connection failure can hit one Binance path while the fallback path still works -> fix: verify the persisted `funding_rate.exchange` / `long_short_ratio.exchange` values and `alerts` before calling the run failed; if Gate filled the fields and the daily memory line was backfilled, treat the cron run as successful with fallback [Task 1]
- symptom: `external_signals_fetcher.py` prints `RequestsDependencyWarning` about `urllib3/chardet/charset_normalizer` compatibility but the saved signals look complete -> cause: this environment can emit a non-fatal `requests` dependency warning during otherwise healthy fetches -> fix: treat the warning as noise unless the fetch or validation actually fails; the real gates are saved JSON content, `--status`, and the daily-memory backfill [Task 1]
- symptom: exit code 0 but uncertain whether the data really refreshed -> cause: console success text can come without a strong persistence check -> fix: inspect the JSON fields, timestamp, size, and fallback markers like `exchange = gate` / `source_note = binance_unreachable_fallback` [Task 1]
- symptom: the task only needs a concise persisted-state summary, not a deep JSON diff -> cause: overusing `jq` or longer field dumps adds noise after the artifact is already known-valid -> fix: use `python3 Knowledge/external_signals/external_signals_fetcher.py --status` plus `stat` as the short proof path, then append the daily memory line [Task 1]
- symptom: a `jq` probe for `fear_greed_index` or `market_sentiment` comes back `null` or misleadingly missing -> cause: the persisted file's real top-level key is `fear_greed` -> fix: inspect `fear_greed` and the actual saved top-level keys before concluding the JSON schema changed or the fetch failed [Task 1]
- symptom: a nested `jq` projection asks for old fields like `avg_rate` or `raw_data` and prints `null` even though the saved file is fresh -> cause: the persisted nested schema now uses `funding_rate.value`, `funding_rate.raw`, `funding_rate.timestamp`, and `long_short_ratio.long_short_ratio` -> fix: inspect `jq '.funding_rate | keys'` and `jq '.long_short_ratio | keys'` first, then read the real saved paths before diagnosing a fetch problem [Task 1]
- symptom: a mixed `jq` pipeline like `jq 'keys, .fear_greed, .fear_greed_index, .funding_rate | keys'` errors even though the saved file is valid -> cause: the probe mixes incompatible shapes and old field names, so `null` values break the pipeline -> fix: prefer `--status` first, then inspect `jq 'keys'` or targeted real paths such as `.funding_rate`, `.long_short_ratio`, `.fear_greed`, and `.alerts` [Task 1]
- symptom: `ps -p <pid>` exits 1 after the fetcher run, so process listing does not confirm completion -> cause: the PID may already be gone or the process check races the finished run, making `ps` weaker than the persisted artifact -> fix: trust `stat`/mtime on `Knowledge/external_signals/external_signals.json` plus `external_signals_fetcher.py --status` and JSON inspection instead of blocking on `ps` output [Task 1]
- symptom: a combined zsh validation command stops before `ls` or `python3 -m json.tool` runs -> cause: `status` is a read-only variable name in zsh -> fix: rename the capture variable to `exit_code` or another non-reserved name before retrying the verification chain [Task 1]
- symptom: `apply_patch` fails while adding the daily memory line -> cause: the expected context in `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` drifted after earlier edits -> fix: reread the file tail or target section first, then patch against the current content instead of retrying the stale hunk [Task 1]
- symptom: the JSON file is fresh and `--status` is healthy, but `memory/2026-05-01.md` still only contains older same-day entries such as `00:06` or stops before the newest rerun -> cause: repeated cron runs do not guarantee their own journal append even when the fetch itself succeeds -> fix: compare the current run timestamp against the active `## 外部信号` block and append the missing `00:13` / `00:17` / `00:22` / `00:25` / `00:36` / `00:42` / `00:49` / `00:55` / `01:06` / `01:12` / `01:48` / `01:57` / `03:06` / `03:12` / `03:51` / `03:55` line immediately instead of assuming one earlier same-day entry is enough [Task 1]

## Failures and how to do differently

- symptom: routine watchdog heartbeat has no anomalies -> cause: healthy `cloudflared` state -> fix: do not over-investigate; append the success note and stay silent unless the workflow requires a brief completion reply [Task 1]
- symptom: watchdog returns non-zero or reports disconnects instead of `近1h断线次数: 0` -> cause: actual connectivity or daemon issue, not a bookkeeping task -> fix: pivot immediately from “check +记账” to investigation instead of writing a normal-success note [Task 1]
- symptom: a cron/watchdog run was reported but not written into `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` -> cause: daily continuity step was skipped, or the check looked only under the wrong heading -> fix: patch the active watchdog section immediately after the command result is known, and if the row is not there, check both `## 工部` and `## Cloudflared Watchdog` before assuming the write failed [Task 1]
- symptom: a first patch attempt reports success but the intended watchdog line still does not appear -> cause: the hunk matched too loosely and became a no-op against the live daily-memory block -> fix: reread the exact surrounding block, apply a precise old/new replacement, and immediately confirm the new timestamp with `grep -n "HH:MM 定时看门狗"` [Task 1]
- symptom: a patch attempt targets the wrong path variant even though the script run was correct -> cause: editing drift between similarly named paths instead of the active workspace copy -> fix: confirm the current cwd and patch `/Users/luxiangnan/.openclaw/workspace-tianlu/memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` directly before retrying the edit [Task 1]
- symptom: `/tmp/cloudflared-watchdog.state` is missing during a healthy run -> cause: this state file is only written when the alert threshold is reached -> fix: do not treat the missing state file as a failure; verify the log recount and `launchctl` status instead if stronger proof is needed [Task 1]
- symptom: watchdog just passed, but the tunnel log tail still shows `/Users/luxiangnan/.cloudflared/restart-wrapper.sh: ... Killed: 9 /opt/homebrew/bin/cloudflared ...` -> cause: historical shutdown/restart noise in the wrapper log, not necessarily a current watchdog failure -> fix: distinguish “watchdog passed right now” from older wrapper restart events, and only escalate if the current run also shows disconnects, non-zero exit, or a non-running `launchctl` state [Task 1]
- symptom: the watchdog script exits `0` and reports `近1h断线次数: 0`, but `memory/2026-05-01.md` still has no current watchdog line such as `00:03` or `00:16` -> cause: the script does not write the journal entry on its own, and a new day may not even have a `## Cloudflared Watchdog` section yet -> fix: grep for the expected timestamp first, create or patch the active watchdog section when absent, then re-verify with `grep` and `stat` before closing [Task 1]
- symptom: an expected watchdog skill file path returns `ENOENT` before the run even starts -> cause: the advertised global skill path is absent in this environment -> fix: pivot immediately to the local memory/runbook plus `bash /Users/luxiangnan/edict/scripts/cloudflared-watchdog.sh` and `launchctl` verification instead of blocking on the missing skill file [Task 1]
- symptom: a quick `/metrics` parse blows up with a Python `SyntaxError` even though the endpoint is healthy -> cause: raw metrics text was piped into Python as source code -> fix: fetch and parse `/metrics` inside Python with `urllib.request`, or inspect the raw endpoint directly instead of piping it into `python -` [Task 1]

## User preferences

- when the cron wrapper says the result can be delivered automatically if no direct message is sent, the workflow can just finish the run and return a concise completion note -> don’t overcomplicate cron callbacks [Task 1]
- when the processor returns no tasks, the user/workflow still expects a timestamped daily log entry -> keep daily summaries continuous even for no-op runs [Task 1]
- when this no-op processor cron finishes, also verify the current `tasks_source.json` state distribution before closing -> don’t rely on stdout alone when the queue is expected to be empty [Task 1]

## Failures and how to do differently

- symptom: `zsh:1: command not found: rg` during environment inspection -> cause: `rg` was unavailable in that run context -> fix: fall back to `find`, `grep`, and `sed` instead of spending time retrying ripgrep-specific workflows [Task 1]
- symptom: no actual processor work happened -> cause: the queue was empty (`processed=0`) -> fix: treat “script ran cleanly + daily summary updated” as the completion condition instead of waiting for downstream task side effects [Task 1]
- symptom: `auto_processor.py` exits cleanly but today’s `## 中书省` line is still missing -> cause: the processor does not always append its own daily-memory record -> fix: grep the expected timestamp first, and if the line is absent use `apply_patch`, then re-grep and `stat` the file to confirm the side effect really landed [Task 1]
- symptom: `auto_processor.py` says `无待处理任务`, but the actual task source state is unknown -> cause: only stdout was checked, so a stale or mismatched queue snapshot could be missed -> fix: re-check `/Users/luxiangnan/edict/data/tasks_source.json` for the current `中书省` / `Taizi` distribution before treating the no-op run as fully verified [Task 1]
